# LOOP MEMORY — Career Operator (cross-run lessons)

Durable lessons for the factory loop. Append dated entries. Keep it honest and short.

---

### 2026-07-19 (run 65) — FULL 8-scout sweep on the deeply-converged repo (~65×). Shipped the MAXIMAL file-disjoint value-bar set: 5 PRs (#445–#449) across mobile a11y, doc honesty, org-billing test-net, and two web load-error/affordance fixes. DROPPED a 6th candidate (coach ceiling-refund) at the maker≠checker gate — an "honesty" refund that would have removed a load-bearing abuse bound.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (c5ceefc = #444, run 64). Branch reset to origin/main. Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + **776 non-live tests @ ~91.8%** (floor 88) + 15 journeys, asgi import OK; web + mobile `tsc --noEmit` + lint green (installed both `node_modules`). Confirmed the 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD's (2026-07-16, overall **B**) two LOOP-buildable A→A+ gaps STAY closed on HEAD (embedding-refund #419; ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT A4/G4/G7 corrected) — did NOT re-do. FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · LLM-honesty · mobile · security · performance · tests-evals · store/doc-honesty · web).

- **[#445 mobile-a11y] Coach Send button disabled on empty input — `mobile/src/app/(tabs)/coach.tsx`.** The Send Pressable was always tappable (disabled only while `sending`) but `send()` no-ops on empty/whitespace — an enabled control that silently does nothing, announced actionable to AT. Gated on `canSend`, 0.5-opacity disabled (the app's one disabled convention: shared `Button` + `team.tsx`), accessibilityState synced. maker≠checker: the design reviewer caught my comment's FALSE "matches the web app" claim (web coach only disables on `sending`) → corrected to cite only the native surfaces that actually do this, AND that catch surfaced the web twin defect → #449.
- **[#446 doc-honesty] README mobile-billing status de-staled — `README.md`.** Status line still said "mobile billing is in progress" — stale since #412 landed the real RevenueCat client + `/api/billing/revenuecat-webhook`. Corrected to "inert pending owner RevenueCat keys + a signed build," matching ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT + mobile/README. maker≠checker: style reviewer caught a verb-object mismatch ("sets … a signed build") → reused the repo's established "pending" idiom.
- **[#447 tests] Org member-removal entitlement net — `tests/test_org_billing.py`.** Two uncovered money/correctness branches on `DELETE /api/org/members`: (1) removing a member who ALSO holds an individual Stripe sub keeps PREMIUM (removal-path recompute — distinct from the org-CANCEL and mobile-sub regressions already present); (2) removing a nonmember returns the honest 404. Both revert-relevant, both APPROVE from 2 reviewers (genuinely uncovered, real nets not tautologies).
- **[#448 web] Settings load-error surfacing — `web/app/app/settings/page.tsx`.** ResumeCard: a failed résumé fetch set `error` but left `resume=null` → infinite skeleton, error unreachable (a silent dead-end on a core surface). GithubEnrichmentCard (folded in from a W1 reviewer): `.catch(setCompetencies([]))` disguised a load failure as "No skills imported yet." Both now surface an honest load error. maker≠checker: design reviewer established the convention — quiet/gray/no-alert for on-MOUNT load failures (team/referral/enrichment), red `ErrorText`/`role=alert` reserved for user-INITIATED action failures — so ResumeCard's load error moved to gray + copy aligned to "Could not … . Try again."
- **[#449 web-a11y] Coach Send button disabled on empty — `web/app/app/coach/page.tsx`.** The web twin of #445, surfaced by #445's reviewer: `disabled={sending || !input.trim()}`. No E2E impact (the only coach journey visits as a free/gated user). 2 reviewers APPROVE.

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT — declined / DROPPED (documented, not scarcity):**
- **[DROPPED at the gate] Coach LLM ceiling-refund on INPUT-moderation short-circuit (`asgi.py`/`career_coach.py`).** The scout framed it as "charging a distressed user a daily-AI slot for a zero-cost canned safety reply." Built + reviewed, then the maker≠checker DESIGN reviewer killed it on TWO grounds: (a) the daily ceiling was the ONLY user-keyed cap on this path — `rate_limit("llm",20)` is IP-keyed — so refunding every moderated turn opens an unbounded `ChatMessage`-write vector (2 rows/turn, victim-scoped, via rotating IPs); (b) it CONTRADICTS the project's deliberate stance that moderation rejections consume the ceiling as an abuse bound (`asgi.py:494-495`; the scoring-path moderation-422 is deliberately NOT refunded). A moderated crisis turn PRODUCES + PERSISTS an artifact — it is not a provider outage (the only legitimate refund class, #419/#336). The gain (1 of 25 daily slots) is net-negative once the DoS regression is priced in. (The correctness reviewer had ALSO caught a separate missed-refund regression from hoisting construction outside the `try` — fixed before the drop decision.) Branch discarded, not shipped.
- **org/members email enumeration (security scout) — DECLINED, re-find of run-63's decline.** `add_member` raises `OrgNotActive` FIRST, so the 404/409 oracle is only reachable on a PAID active org; the distinct admin messages have genuine usability and anonymous surfaces are already enumeration-defended. Below the bar (unchanged from run 63).
- **GitHub-enrichment 15s sync call (perf scout) — DECLINED.** Bounded < the 60s budget, user-initiated import with a spinner; a queue/async rewrite is a big lift for marginal gain on a one-shot action.
- **RevenueCat webhook out-of-order re-grant (backend scout) — DECLINED.** A real defense-in-depth gap, but the clean fix needs a DB column + migration for a feature that is INERT until the owner sets keys — migration risk > current (zero) impact. Recorded for when mobile billing goes live.
- **org_billing lock-None / IntegrityError-masking (backend scout ×2) — DECLINED.** The FK constraint already prevents the actual corruption; the residual is a wrong error string on an owner-deletes-own-account-mid-request race. Below the bar.
- **mobile coach-suggestions silent-empty (mobile scout) — DECLINED, re-find of run-63's decline.** Suggestions are optional prompt chips; the coach is fully functional on failure ("Ask me anything…") with no user DATA lost. Correct graceful degrade.

**CONVERGENCE READ (~65× at the build waterline).** Both ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked (business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B DATA; store-readiness needs a signed native build for screenshots). No DoD box flips — pure a11y/correctness/doc-honesty/test-net hardening. Readiness honestly NOT met/attempted. **LESSON: a refund that reads as an honesty win can DELETE a load-bearing abuse bound. Before giving back a consumed rate/spend slot, check two things: (1) is that slot ALSO the only USER-keyed cap on a persisted side-effect (here `ChatMessage` writes, since the sibling rate limiter is IP-keyed)? and (2) does the project DELIBERATELY count the rejected class (moderation) as an abuse signal elsewhere (the scoring path's non-refunded 422)? If either holds, the value bar is net-of-regression and a 1-slot fairness gain loses to an unbounded-write DoS. The correctness review can pass while the DESIGN review kills the change — run both.**

### 2026-07-19 (run 64) — FULL 8-scout sweep on the deeply-converged repo (~64×). Shipped 3 file-disjoint value-bar changes in ONE branch-constrained PR: a mobile silent-data-loss fix + an org-webhook N+1 kill + a doc self-contradiction/orphaned-artifact cleanup. 5 of 8 scout surfaces returned ZERO; 2 backend RACE candidates verified BELOW-BAR and declined.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (ce7377d = #443, run 63). Branch reset to origin/main. Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + **774 non-live tests @ ~91.8%** (floor 88), asgi import OK; mobile `tsc --noEmit` + `expo lint` + jest (87) green (installed `mobile/node_modules`). Confirmed the 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD's (2026-07-16, overall **B**) two LOOP-buildable A→A+ gaps STAY closed on HEAD (embedding-refund #419; ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT A4/G4/G7 corrected) — did NOT re-do. FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · billing · web · mobile · security · tests-evals/doc-honesty · performance · artifact/quality-reconcile); web + security + billing returned ZERO.

- **[r64-mobile] Learning-plan silent data loss on REGENERATE — `mobile/src/app/(tabs)/insights.tsx` + `mobile/__tests__/insights-screen.test.tsx`.** `generatePlan` called `setPlan(null)` BEFORE the request, so a transient 5xx on a *regenerate* silently DESTROYED the user's already-generated (session-only, never-persisted) plan — the same silent-data-loss class as run-62 #439 (`setCompetencies([])`). The render already hides the plan while `planLoading`, so the pre-clear had zero visual benefit; removing it matches the house pattern in `job/[id].tsx` `generateStudyPlan` (never pre-clears). Load-bearing test asserts a failed regenerate keeps the plan (button stays "Regenerate plan", not "Generate learning plan"); revert-proven ✓/✕.
- **[r64-perf] Org-webhook tier-reconcile N+1 — `src/org_billing.py` (`_recompute_all_member_tiers`) + `tests/test_perf_n1.py`.** Ran a per-member `SELECT … FROM users` inside a loop on the SYNCHRONOUS Stripe org-webhook path (seat created/updated/deleted), so a large org (up to MAX_SEATS) fired 1 + N round-trips against the 60s serverless budget. Now one `User.id.in_(...)` bulk load. Regression test counts ONLY `FROM users` statements (recompute_user_tier reads subscriptions/org_members, never users — unconfounded) and asserts a CONSTANT single bulk load for 2 and 5 members; revert-proven (per-member loop → `2 != 1`). Semantic parity: `uq_org_member_user` UNIQUE(user_id) means no dedupe/dup risk; missing-user skip preserved by `.in_()` omission; `if not members: return` is a pure no-op. Same class as run-62 #437.
- **[r64-docs] BRAND_KIT self-contradiction + orphaned route-inventory — `docs/brand/BRAND_KIT.md` + deleted `docs/ROUTE_INVENTORY.md`.** BRAND_KIT's "Consistency items" section still called the app icon "still the Expo template assets / owner-designer work" — contradicting its OWN "App icon/splash" row (bespoke chevron-"A", committed), the code (`mobile/assets/images/icon.png`), ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT G7, and the scorecard. Corrected to state the icon is the committed bespoke mark; the one remaining store-listing artifact gap is screenshots (Human-Core signed build). Also deleted the orphaned, stale, untested duplicate root `docs/ROUTE_INVENTORY.md` (48 routes, missing 2 real ones) — the canonical, test-guarded inventory is `docs/ci/ROUTE_INVENTORY.md` (only historical loop-memory prose references the old path).

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT — declined (documented, not scarcity):**
- **create_job idempotency dup-race (backend scout BUG#1) — DECLINED.** Concurrent identical POSTs *can* create duplicate JobPosting rows (no UNIQUE on user/title/company/url, only a non-unique `ix_job_user_company` Index), but a proper fix needs a SCHEMA MIGRATION on live Neon (data-migration risk) AND wouldn't even catch the NULL-url case (Postgres treats NULLs as distinct); run 62 already assessed this race as over-framed/not-reachable-live. The realistic trigger (double-submit) yields a deletable cosmetic duplicate, NOT data loss/spend/security. Below the bar vs. the migration risk.
- **free-tier job-cap lost-update (backend scout BUG#2) — DECLINED.** `check_usage_limits` reads the count then `increment_job_usage` does a non-atomic ORM `+= 1`, so concurrent requests at the boundary can let a free user track a handful of extra jobs. But the REAL wallet-drain (paid Gemini embeddings) is ALREADY atomic via the DB-backed `score_daily` SELECT..FOR UPDATE ceiling — this leak grants no paid feature and no spend; it's bounded + self-heals on the next sequential request. A clean fix means an invasive row-lock/atomic-conditional refactor of the hot job-add monetization path that can't be load-tested on Linux. Risk/reward below the bar.
- **web + security + billing scouts: ZERO findings.** Triangulation on a deeply-hardened repo, not artificial scarcity. Artifact scout's orphaned root ROUTE_INVENTORY was folded into the docs change; its self-rated below-bar status was overridden only because deleting a false-claiming living artifact is genuine artifact integrity.

**CONVERGENCE READ (~64× at the build waterline).** Both ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked (business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B DATA; store-readiness needs a signed native build for screenshots). No DoD box flips — pure data-loss/perf/doc-honesty hardening. Readiness honestly NOT met/attempted. **LESSON: on a converged repo the highest-yield backend scout findings are RACES — and most dissolve on the value bar, not on reachability: BUG#1 was reachable but needed a risky schema migration for a cosmetic dup; BUG#2 was a real lost-update but the money it "protects" is already atomic elsewhere, so the leak is worthless to an attacker. Trace where the ACTUAL cost/spend is gated before pricing a monetization-boundary race — the fix's blast radius on the hot path often exceeds the leak's value.**

### 2026-07-19 (run 63) — FULL 8-scout sweep on the deeply-converged repo (~63×). Shipped 3 file-disjoint value-bar changes in ONE branch-constrained PR: a perf bound + a compliance regression net + a stale agent-doc rewrite. 5 of 8 scout surfaces returned ZERO; the 3 real findings all revert-proven load-bearing; 2 candidates verified BELOW the bar and declined.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (391d59a = #442, run 62 bookkeeping; branch in sync 0/0). Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + **772 non-live tests @ ~91.8%** (floor 88), asgi import OK; mobile `tsc --noEmit` green (installed `mobile/node_modules`). Confirmed the 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD's (2026-07-16, overall **B**) two LOOP-buildable A→A+ gaps are ALREADY closed on HEAD (correctness embedding-refund + stale ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT both fixed by #419, re-verified `asgi.py:1597` refund + A4/G4/G7 corrected) — did NOT re-do. FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · billing · web · mobile · security · tests-evals · performance · artifact-freshness/quality-reconcile); backend + billing + web returned ZERO.

- **[r63-perf] Bounded the mock-interviews list — `asgi.py` (`list_mock_interviews`) + `tests/test_mock_interview.py`.** `GET /api/prep/mock-interviews` used an unbounded `.all()` while EVERY sibling list endpoint is capped (`_JOBS_LIST_DEFAULT_LIMIT`/`_SKILL_GAP_JOB_CAP`=500). Each `MockInterview` row carries its questions + per-answer scores as JSON, so a heavy user's sessions on one job would all load into memory + serialize on a hot authed read — inflating serverless p99 / OOM risk. Bounded to `_MOCK_INTERVIEWS_LIST_CAP=200` most-recent. New test seeds 5, monkeypatches the cap to 3, asserts exactly the 3 most-recent in desc order. LOAD-BEARING (revert-proven by the maker AND both reviewers: dropping `.limit(...)` returns 5 → reddens). Both web + mobile callers just render the list (no total-count claim), so no silent-lie about totals — consistent with the codebase's existing silent-cap convention.
- **[r63-compliance] Consent-REVOCATION enforcement regression net — `tests/test_ai_consent.py`.** The consent gate's *revocation* enforcement was UNTESTED: `test_consent_state_round_trip` only proved the `ai_consent_at` flag toggles. A regression that read consent from a login-time CACHE (instead of re-checking per request) would keep AI usable after revocation while every existing consent test stayed GREEN — a silent Apple 5.1.2(i) revocability break. New test pins grant→generate(reached)→revoke→same endpoint 403 `ai_consent_required` with NO post-revoke generation. LOAD-BEARING + isolates the gate as the sole 403 cause (user made Premium so the free prep-pack quota can't confound; the ceiling raises a plain-string 429, not the `{code}` dict asserted). Revert-proven: disabling `require_ai_consent` reddens it while the flag-toggle test stays GREEN (exactly the regression class). maker≠checker polish: Reviewer A flagged the post-revoke `calls["n"]==1` as no-independent-signal → strengthened `_boom` to bump the same counter so "no generation after revoke" is asserted independently of the status code.
- **[r63-artifact] Refreshed the severely-stale `CLAUDE.MD`.** It still described an "Initial Setup" web-scraper with "no source files created yet / only .git/" — actively-WRONG context on an AGENT ENTRY-POINT file for a 62-run mature FastAPI+Next.js+Expo product. Rewritten as a concise, accurate orientation pointer to the authoritative docs (AGENTS.md, ROADMAP, VISION, FACTORY_STANDARD, README) + the real stack/gate. Both reviewers cross-checked every claim against the code/dirs/DoD: honest "pre-launch" framing, no overclaim, no dangling doc refs.

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT — declined (documented, not scarcity):**
- **org/members email enumeration (security scout) — DECLINED, scout's exploit precondition is FALSE.** The scout claimed "create a FREE account + FREE org + probe emails" distinguishes registered (409) vs not (404). But `org_billing.add_member` raises `OrgNotActive` FIRST (`src/org_billing.py:166`) — so `MemberNotFound`/`AlreadyInAnotherOrg` are ONLY reachable when the org is ACTIVE, i.e. the attacker must have PURCHASED seats via real Stripe. A paid-subscription-gated oracle where the distinct messages ("no account exists" vs "already in another org") have genuine admin usability, and the anonymous high-value surfaces (register/login) are already enumeration-defended. Collapsing them is a net UX regression against a threat that already paid. Below the value bar.
- **mobile résumé/enrichment "Reopen Settings" text vs a Retry BUTTON + coach-suggestion silent-empty (mobile scout ×3) — DECLINED.** The résumé/enrichment cards ALREADY surface an honest error with a documented recovery path (the run-62 pattern) — not a dead-end; a Retry button is polish, not value-bar-clearing. Coach *suggestions* are optional prompt chips: on failure the coach is fully functional ("Ask me anything…") with no user-DATA lost — correct graceful degrade, not the run-62 enrichment `setCompetencies([])` data-loss class (which erased the user's OWN skills). Below the bar.
- **tests-evals per-PR live-model smoke (artifact/quality-reconcile scout) — DECLINED, non-ship-critical + owner/CI-blocked.** Adding a per-PR live Gemini smoke needs a `.github/` CI change (owner-only) OR making a flaky, money-spending live call block PRs; the scorecard itself marks tests-evals NON-ship-critical and the nightly cadence is a deliberate accepted decision (multiple prior runs). No change.
- **backend + billing + web scouts: ZERO findings.** Triangulation on a deeply-hardened repo, not artificial scarcity.

**CONVERGENCE READ (~63× at the build waterline).** Both ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked (business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B DATA; store-readiness needs a signed native build for screenshots). No DoD box flips — this run was pure perf/compliance/artifact hardening. Readiness honestly NOT met/attempted. No recurring wall → no harness proposal. **LESSON: before accepting a security scout's "enumeration" finding, TRACE the exception ORDER in the underlying function — an oracle gated behind a check that fires FIRST (here `OrgNotActive` before any email lookup) has a far higher precondition than the scout's scenario assumes (a PAID active org, not a free one), which can move it below the value bar. And a "no side-effect fired" test assertion must touch the SAME observable the side-effect would (bump the shared counter in the sentinel), or it asserts nothing.**

### 2026-07-18 (run 62) — FULL 8-scout sweep. Shipped the MAXIMAL file-disjoint value-bar set: 5 PRs (#437–#441) across correctness+perf, eval-strengthening, mobile honest-degrade, mobile a11y, and living-artifact freshness. maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP hard — #437 took two review cycles to fix a vacuous test + an inefficient re-read it originally shipped.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (bdb5087 = #436). Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + **769 non-live tests @ ~91.8%** (floor 88), asgi import OK; mobile `tsc`+`expo lint`+jest baseline green (installed `mobile/node_modules`). The 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD (2026-07-16, overall **B**) named several LOOP-buildable A→A+ gaps that a quality-reconcile check confirmed ALREADY CLOSED on HEAD (correctness embedding-refund + stale ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT both fixed by #419; icon bespoke) — did NOT re-do. FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · billing · web · mobile · security · tests-evals · performance · artifact-freshness); security + a broad billing pass returned ZERO findings (repo deeply hardened).

- **[r62-#437] Job-write path: N+1 kill + defensive concurrent-PATCH guard — `asgi.py` (`update_job_status`, `create_job`) + `tests/test_perf_n1.py` + `tests/test_jobs_endpoint.py`.** `job_public()` reads application+score+company; both endpoints serialized an EXPIRED job after commit → 3 lazy round-trips on the hot pipeline-write path. Re-read once with `joinedload` filtered on the path param / a PK captured before commit (never the expired `job.id`, which forces a wasted refresh SELECT). Removed the now-dead `db.refresh(job)` in create_job. Measured engine-level (spans the commit): PATCH tail **7→4**, add-path **→12**. Also a DEFENSIVE (schema-permitted, not-live) IntegrityError guard on the create-Application branch, matching join_waitlist/billing_webhook. **CLOSES the run-26/#266 deferred item** ("re-fetch with joinedload / drop refresh+lazy + a RELIABLE cross-commit query-count test"). **maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP (2 cycles):** cycle-1 BOTH reviewers caught (a) the PATCH perf test was VACUOUS — `_count_queries` binds to a Connection captured before the mid-call commit, so it silently stopped counting exactly where the N+1 lives and passed even when reverted; (b) filtering the re-read on the expired `job.id` added a refresh SELECT (5, not 1); (c) create_job's new path had ZERO coverage; (d) the race was over-framed as a live bug (create_job always makes the Application in the same txn → not reachable today). Fixed all four (new `_count_engine_queries` engine-level counter, filter on param/captured id, added create_job coverage, honest defensive framing); cycle-2 A2 re-verified every fix by reversion, B2's sole ask was a PR-description number sync (14→"≥2 more"), done.
- **[r62-#438] Eval strengthening (§26) — `tests/evals/test_scoring_evals.py`.** `test_extract_skills` asserted a SUBSET (`{python,react,postgresql} <= found`), which tolerates a false-positive regression (a new spurious skill wouldn't break `<=`). The extractor feeds BOTH paid fit-scoring AND the public `/demo`, so a false-positive burst degrades the core value signal (the "obviously-AI/inaccurate" counter-signal). Pinned the EXACT set `{python,react,sql,postgresql}` (sql is a substring match ⊂ postgresql — documented so a future word-boundary refactor reddens + gets reviewed).
- **[r62-#439] Mobile honest-degrade — `mobile/src/app/(tabs)/settings.tsx`.** The GitHub-enrichment card did `setCompetencies([])` on a `getEnrichment()` load failure — indistinguishable from "no skills imported", so a Pro user's imported skills silently VANISH on a transient failure. Keep competencies null + surface an honest error, mirroring the résumé card. Regression test verified load-bearing (fails on the old `[]` path).
- **[r62-#440] Mobile a11y — `mobile/src/app/interview/[jobId].tsx`.** Past-session rows (a Pressable + two child Text) had only `accessibilityRole=button`; child-text aggregation on a Pressable is platform-dependent, so a screen reader may announce a bare "button" on the flagship mock-interview surface. Added an explicit `accessibilityLabel` (status + progress + action as one row). Test verified load-bearing.
- **[r62-#441] Living-artifact freshness — `mobile/README.md`.** The status section understated the biggest shipped mobile feature: it listed IAP as unbuilt though the RevenueCat client landed (#412), and grouped icon/feature-graphic/screenshots under one ⏳ though the bespoke icon + feature graphic are committed. Corrected to match code + ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT (client built + inert-when-unkeyed; only screenshots remain, Human-Core). Both reviewers fact-checked every claim.

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT — declined/dissolved (documented, not scarcity):**
- **Performance async Margin telemetry (scorecard A→A+, perf scout) — declined AGAIN, correct-as-is.** The perf scout re-confirmed every off-hot-path option (BackgroundTasks / response.background / queue) is killed by Vercel's return-time freeze — moving it would LOSE telemetry (a regression disguised as a fix). The synchronous, 1.0s-bounded design (#389) is deliberate. Not value-bar-clearing.
- **Mobile billing webhook idempotency test (billing scout) — declined as padding.** The code is naturally idempotent (UPDATE-only, no insert-race) with no current bug; a parity test for already-correct code with no associated fix is closer to padding than §26 coverage.
- **Web copy-button loading state / mobile coach "Not now" / interview 0-question guard — marginal/impossible-case, dropped.** Idempotent DELETE (double-click harmless), OS back available, server bounds questions 3–8. Below the value bar.
- **security scout: ZERO findings; broad billing scout: 1 finding (the padding test above).** Triangulation, not artificial scarcity.

**CONVERGENCE READ (~53× at the build waterline).** Both ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked (business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B DATA; store-readiness needs a signed native build for screenshots). This run was pure quality/correctness/a11y/honesty hardening + one real perf win — no DoD box flips. Readiness honestly NOT met/attempted. No recurring wall → no harness proposal. **LESSON (the run's headline): a query-count regression test that attaches its listener to a single Connection is VACUOUS for any endpoint that commits mid-call — the connection is swapped after commit and the listener goes blind exactly where the post-commit N+1 lives. Count on the ENGINE (`db.get_bind()`) to span the commit, and always prove a perf guard is load-bearing by reverting the fix. This is the run-26/#266 trap; it is now closed with a reliable counter.**

### 2026-07-18 (run 61) — FULL 8-scout sweep. Advanced the LOWEST INCOMPLETE substantive ROADMAP item (Track C seat-tier MOBILE management surface, line 301) + 4 file-disjoint value-bar changes. One PR (branch-constrained). Scorecard's stale loop-buildable gaps re-confirmed already-closed; only owner/native/market gaps remain there.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (a0b06ea = #428, run 60 = this branch's base, in sync 0/0). Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + **761 non-live tests @ ~91.8%** (floor 88), asgi import OK; mobile `tsc --noEmit` + `expo lint` baseline green (installed `mobile/node_modules` to gate the native work LOCALLY, not just on CI). The 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD (2026-07-16, overall **B**) is STALE on two dims: its correctness A→A+ (embedding-outage refund) is ALREADY closed (asgi.py:1576/1598 + `test_scorer_degradation.py`) and its artifact-integrity/store `ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT.md` stale-doc gap is ALREADY fixed (A4/G4 read OPEN, G7 = bespoke icon) — a quality-reconcile scout confirmed both against HEAD; did NOT re-do. - **[r61-A] Track C seat-tier MOBILE management surface — `mobile/src/app/team.tsx` (new) + `mobile/src/services/api.ts` (getOrg/addOrgMember/removeOrgMember) + `mobile/src/types.ts` (Organization/OrgMember) + `_layout.tsx` route + a Settings "Team" card.** The web half landed run 42 (#356); the mobile half was the explicit remaining gap. Harm is one duplicate job + one of 25 daily slots, rare trigger. Wrong risk/reward.

### 2026-07-17 (run 59) — Shipped ONE genuine value-bar change: a §26 billing-webhook CONCURRENT-insert-race hardening (fail-closed retry-as-update). Initially BUILT the four Track G/H engine items (publishing-queue, experiment-engine, ASO/SEO plan, launch-plan doc) through review — then DROPPED all four unshipped on recognizing they are the STANDING §9 PMF-first deferral (LOOP_HEALTH `deferred_decisions`, ~45×, run-50 precedent). The billing fix passed maker≠checker after BOTH reviewers caught real BLOCKING defects.

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (51f9afa = #420, run 58, this branch's base). Deps installed; baseline flake8 clean + 750 non-live tests @ ~91.8% (floor 88), asgi import OK. FULL 7-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · security/abuse · web+mobile functional · + 4 Track G/H build-scope scouts). Product deeply converged: web+mobile functional scout ZERO, security scout ZERO. Backend-correctness scout surfaced 2 candidates.

- **[r59-1] Billing-webhook concurrent-insert-race hardening — `asgi.py` billing_webhook + `tests/test_billing.py` (new test), the ONE shipped change.** VERIFIED real + distinct from run-58's SEQUENTIAL redelivery test: two near-simultaneous FIRST deliveries of the same event both SELECT no Subscription row + INSERT → the loser trips `subscriptions.user_id` UNIQUE → IntegrityError. Fix: wrap the WHOLE apply+commit in a 2-attempt retry-as-update loop; on the 2nd failure log + re-raise (FAIL CLOSED → Stripe re-delivers). Safe because `apply_event` is idempotent (SELECT-then-upsert + deterministic recompute_user_tier). **maker≠checker CAUGHT TWO REAL BLOCKING DEFECTS (both fixed pre-merge):** (A, Reviewer A) my first cut wrapped ONLY `db.commit()` — but `_upsert_subscription` does an explicit `db.flush()`, so the REAL race raises IntegrityError at FLUSH *inside* `apply_event` (empirically confirmed), which the commit-only try didn't cover → the genuine race would still 500; AND my test injected at commit, so it passed regardless (not load-bearing). Fixed: try now wraps the whole apply+commit; test injects at FLUSH (revert-verified: narrowing the try back to commit-only turns it RED). (B, Reviewer B) if BOTH attempts raise IntegrityError the loop fell through to `return {"received": True}` — a FAKE 200 that makes Stripe STOP retrying and silently drops entitlement (worse than the original self-healing 500). Fixed: fail closed on the 2nd failure. **LESSONS: (1) a premature `flush()` moves where an IntegrityError surfaces — scope the try to the whole write, not just commit; (2) an exhausted retry must FAIL CLOSED, never return success with nothing committed; (3) a race test must inject the fault where the DB actually raises (flush), or it isn't load-bearing.**

- **[r59-DROP] Built then DROPPED the four Track G/H engine items — the §9 PMF-first PADDING failure mode.** I built publishing-queue (`src/publishing`, dry-run seam + DB model + migration), experiment-engine (`src/experiments`, min-sample-gated evaluator), and the ASO/SEO + launch-plan docs, and took them through 2 Sonnet reviewers (who caught + I fixed a real Wilson-interval `sqrt(negative)` crash — proportion test invalid for unbounded count-per-signup data — and a flush-scope bug). Then, reading LOOP_HEALTH `deferred_decisions` (line ~46), I found these EXACT items are a STANDING, ~45×-reaffirmed, condition-gated §9 PMF-first deferral: "SPECULATIVE pre-launch infra (0 users/0 channels)… Reopens ONLY on first users / a connected channel, not on code readiness," and **RUN 50 did EXACTLY this — built them clean, review-passed, then DROPPED unshipped**. Conditions are UNCHANGED (GROWTH_STATUS: pre_launch, 0 users, `channels_connected: []`, `pmf.signal: none`). So shipping them is the PADDING failure mode the mandate forbids, regardless of code quality — an experiment engine has no users to experiment on; a publishing queue has no channel/audience. DROPPED all four + their bookkeeping (engine_pct stays 50). **LESSON (the run-50 lesson, re-learned the hard way): READ `LOOP_HEALTH.deferred_decisions` BEFORE building any Track G/H infra item. A clean, review-passed prototype does NOT override a standing, condition-gated PMF-first deferral; only a CHANGE in the gating condition (first users / a connected channel) reopens it. The scout sweep found the specs "buildable" but buildability ≠ value-bar-clearing under §9.**

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT — the 2nd correctness candidate DISSOLVED:**
- **Window-rollover refund (backend scout finding #2) — DECLINED, documented-intended.** `_refund_counter` recomputes `window_key = time()//86400` at refund time, so a request spanning midnight refunds the WRONG (new) window. But `_refund_counter`'s OWN docstring (asgi.py:353-355) already documents this as a deliberate harmless no-op, and there is NO user harm: the old window resets to a fresh full ceiling at midnight regardless, so the "lost" refund is in a window that no longer meters anything. Not a bug.

The 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD (2026-07-16, overall **B**, ship_gate NO) had its two LOOP-buildable A→A+ top_gaps (correctness embedding-refund + artifact-integrity ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT staleness) BOTH actioned by #419 LAST run — reconciled before touching anything, did NOT re-do. FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep: backend-correctness · security/abuse · web functional+design · mobile Expo/RN · tests-evals · artifact-freshness · performance/efficiency · monetization+functional-reality.

- **[r58-1] §26 regression net — Stripe-webhook redelivery idempotency (`tests/test_billing.py`, file-DISJOINT).** Stripe redelivers webhook events (retries on any non-2xx / network blip / at-least-once delivery), so the SAME signed `checkout.session.completed` can legitimately arrive more than once — but NO test delivered a VALID event twice (the existing forged-sig test fails the HMAC check, and the run-53 replay test fails the ancient-TIMESTAMP tolerance window — BOTH bail before `apply_event` ever runs, so the upsert-idempotency path was unexercised). New `test_webhook_redelivered_checkout_is_idempotent_one_subscription_row` posts the same signed event TWICE and asserts 200 both times + tier PREMIUM + EXACTLY ONE `Subscription` row. Two layers guarantee idempotency (nothing pinned EITHER): app-level `_upsert_subscription` keeps one row per user (SELECT-then-create-if-absent → clean UPDATE on redelivery), and DB-level `Subscription.user_id` is `unique=True` (defense-in-depth). LOAD-BEARING (revert-verified by the maker AND both reviewers independently): a blind `db.add(Subscription(...))` refactor trips the unique constraint on the 2nd delivery → `IntegrityError` → the webhook 500s (Stripe retries forever, entitlement bookkeeping breaks) → the test reddens. **MAKER SELF-CAUGHT overclaim (before reviewers finished):** my first docstring said the blind-add regression "would silently create duplicate audit rows" — FALSE: the `user_id` unique constraint turns it into a LOUD IntegrityError→500, not silent duplication. Discovered by reading the schema; corrected the docstring to the real failure mode pre-merge. Both Sonnet reviewers INDEPENDENTLY reproduced the same overclaim class and confirmed the final committed docstring is accurate. **LESSON:** before claiming a "silent" corruption failure mode, check the SCHEMA — a unique constraint converts a silent dup into a loud crash, which changes both the failure mode AND how the test catches it (here: via the 2nd delivery's 200-assert, not just the row count).
- **[r58-2] §14 living-doc honesty (`ROADMAP.md:281`, folded into the bookkeeping half of the PR).** The Track-B annotation read ``tests/test_mobile_billing.py`: 12 cases` but the file has 15 test fns / **21 collected** cases (the "12" matched NEITHER honest count). Corrected 12→21 (collected, matching the "cases" wording convention — run-53/54 precedent). Whole-class spot-check: no other `N cases` callout in ROADMAP needed correcting (only one such annotation exists).

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT DISSOLVED 3 OF 4 SCOUT CANDIDATES (the run's headline — false positives caught before writing any code; NOT artificial scarcity, since the real change WAS found + shipped, and NOT padding, since each decline is a named decision):**
- **parse_job_description bare `json.loads` (tests-evals scout #4) — UNWIRED.** The method has NO route caller (`grep` confirmed: routes call the 8 `generate_*`/`score_*` methods, never this). Fixing/testing an unreachable helper is padding (score_all_jobs / get_session_summary precedent). The reachable `json.loads(None)`-on-empty case is ALREADY guarded by `_call_llm`'s empty-response fail-loud (`llm_workflows.py:145`). Its 3 siblings guard json.loads because they ARE wired; this one isn't.
- **mobile avg-score 0→"—" (mobile scout #1) — MIRRORS WEB INTENTIONALLY.** `web/app/app/page.tsx:70` uses the IDENTICAL `average_score ? … : '—'` pattern. The server sends `0.0` as the NO-SCORED-JOBS default (`asgi.py:2733`, `avg_raw is None → 0.0`), so `0`→"—" is the MORE honest display (a real 0-avg needs every scored job rounding to ~0, extraordinarily rare). A blanket `!= null` fix would show "0" when nothing is scored (LESS honest) AND diverge from web (a design-taste/parity regression). Genuinely distinguishing needs a server `scored_count` field — cross-cutting, not a one-liner. Not a bug on either platform.
- **org_billing `_recompute_all_member_tiers` N+1 (performance scout) — PARTIAL FIX, doesn't clear the bar.** Batching the User fetch leaves `recompute_user_tier`'s own per-user entitlement queries (`_has_active_org_seat`/`_has_active_individual_sub`), so the webhook stays O(N); a full batch is architecturally invasive on `billing.py`'s single-source-of-truth entitlement authority — for an INFREQUENT, 200-seat-capped webhook already well under the 60s budget. Micro-opt, wrong risk/reward.

### 2026-07-16 (run 57) — Actioned the 8th QUALITY_SCORECARD's two loop-buildable A→A+ top_gaps: (1) correctness — refund the score_daily slot on a Gemini embedding OUTAGE; (2) artifact-integrity/store-readiness — corrected the STALE ACCEPTANCE_AUDIT. 2 file-DISJOINT changes + bookkeeping, one PR. maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP (Reviewer A caught a real wallet-drain weakening in my first cut → fixed → fresh re-review APPROVE).

**RUN-START SYNC.** Main GREEN at start (9a574a8 = #418, the 8th audit; this branch's base). Deps installed; local baseline flake8 clean + 748 non-live tests @ 91.80% (floor 88), asgi import smoke OK. 8th audit (2026-07-16) holds overall **B**, ship_gate NO, on two ship-critical dims below A: store-readiness **B** + business-case **B** (both owner/market-blocked). FULL 5-scout Haiku sweep (backend-correctness · security/abuse · web functional+design · tests-evals · artifact-freshness): 4 returned clean/convergence-confirmed; the tests-evals scout INDEPENDENTLY ranked the embedding-refund gap #1 (the exact item I was already fixing) — strong triangulation, not padding.

- **[r57-1] incident/decision — correctness A→A+ (score_daily refund on embedding OUTAGE; `src/ranking/scorer.py` + `asgi.py` + 2 test files, file-DISJOINT from the doc).** `create_job` consumes a per-day `score_daily` embedding slot up front, but `score_job` swallows an embedding failure and degrades to the neutral 0.5 baseline WITHOUT re-raising, so the outer except never fired and the paid slot was silently burned for a call that cost nothing — contradicting the project's own refund principle (count calls that cost money, not outages; `refund_llm_ceiling` honors it on every other paid path). Fix: `JobScorer` exposes `embedding_failed`; `create_job` refunds via `_refund_counter` AFTER the commit (so the refund's own commit only persists the decrement — the job/Application/usage rows are already durable, dodging the transaction-split hazard the consume-first ordering guards). Best-effort (§32): a refund failure never aborts the job add. **maker≠checker CATCH (Reviewer A, REQUEST_CHANGES — genuine security defect):** my first cut set `embedding_failed=True` on ANY exception in `score_job`'s embedding try — but that `try` wraps TWO separately-billed Gemini calls (`ensure_user_embedding` then `ensure_job_embedding`). If the résumé embedding BILLED successfully and then the JD embedding 502'd, I refunded the whole slot despite real spend — a wallet-drain WEAKENING (an attacker crafts JDs that fail the 2nd call post-billing for unlimited refunded adds; the JD is attacker-controlled text). FIX: count billable calls that actually RETURNED (`self._billable_embeddings`, incremented in `get_embedding` after a successful `embeddings.create`, reset per `score_job`); refund ONLY when that count is 0. Correctly handles the cache-hit matrix (résumé cache-hit + JD fail = 0 billable → honest refund; résumé billed + JD fail = 1 → no refund). Fresh re-reviewer APPROVE (walked the 5-case matrix, revert-verified the new security test is uniquely load-bearing). **LESSON:** before reusing a broad `except` scope to make a BILLING decision, check how many separately-billed calls it spans — a signal that conflates "no call made" with "a call billed then a later one failed" weakens the exact ceiling it means to keep honest. Regression nets (all revert-verified load-bearing): `test_embedding_outage_refunds_the_scoring_slot` (integration: ceiling stays clear under repeated outage), `test_no_refund_signal_when_one_embedding_billed_before_a_later_failure` (the security case), + `embedding_failed` assertions on the 3 scorer degradation paths.

### 2026-07-16 (run 55) — FULL 8-scout Haiku sweep on the deeply-converged codebase → shipped ONE PR = 2 file-DISJOINT §26 regression nets (rate-counter insert-race retry + `_enriched_context` paid-path degradation) + bookkeeping. 2 Sonnet reviewers + 1 fresh re-reviewer; both reviewers INDEPENDENTLY caught the same real defect (fixed pre-merge).

**RUN-START SYNC (the standing rule) — reconciled the 07-13 QUALITY_SCORECARD against `git log b221a03..HEAD` before touching anything.** Its LOOP-buildable A→A+ top_gaps already shipped after its grading HEAD (performance/Margin-timeout #389, artifact-integrity/ROUTE_INVENTORY #390). Remaining A→A+ gaps are owner-keyed (tests-evals CI-liveness → GEMINI in CI; security → TURNSTILE_SECRET; design → native captures). Both ship-critical dims (store-readiness C, business-case-strength B) stay owner/market-blocked. Did NOT re-do already-shipped work (no padding). Main GREEN at run-start (bfa4012 = #408, this branch's base — verified via GitHub API); local baseline flake8 clean, 744 non-live tests green (floor 88), import smoke OK.

- **Rate-counter insert-race retry regression net (`tests/test_rate_counter.py`, file-DISJOINT).** `asgi._consume_counter`'s `except IntegrityError: rollback; continue` branch (the cross-instance rate-limit / LLM spend-ceiling **wallet-drain** defense's concurrency handling) had NO coverage — a two-instance insert race on the same (subject,bucket,window) surfaces as a unique-violation the loser must roll back + retry-as-UPDATE, never a 500. Added a deterministic, faithful simulation: freeze the clock so the window key is fixed, make the first commit discard the losing insert + durably commit a WINNER row + raise IntegrityError, so the retry's SELECT finds the winner and takes the UPDATE path → final `count == 2` (winner's 1 + our retried +1). LOAD-BEARING: removing the retry makes the call raise IntegrityError; a naive re-insert would leave count==1, so `==2` also pins that the retry hit the update branch. 40-run soak = 0 failures (deterministic).
- **`_enriched_context` paid-path degradation regression net (`tests/test_github_enrichment.py`, file-DISJOINT).** `LLMWorkflows._enriched_context`'s `except Exception: return ""` (defense-in-depth around resolving the user's link-enriched skills — folded into the PAID prep-pack/cover-letter/tailored-résumé/study-plan/negotiation prompts) had no coverage. Added a test that patches `github_enricher.user_enriched_skills` (the name `_enriched_context` re-imports at call time) to raise and asserts `_enriched_context` returns "" — an optional enrichment lookup can NEVER break a paid generation. LOAD-BEARING (revert-verified red without the except).

**maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP (both reviewers, INDEPENDENTLY, same real defect → fixed → fresh re-review).** My first cut of the rate-counter test used a single-session mock that raised IntegrityError on the first commit WITHOUT a real competing row — so on the retry the SELECT still found None and the code did a second INSERT (count stayed 1), NOT the `row.count += 1` UPDATE path the docstring claimed ("retried as update / the row now exists"). Both reviewers instrumented `db.add` / traced the branch and caught the overclaim; both preferred rewriting it as a genuine race. Did the stronger fix (winner-commit → retry hits the real update branch → count==2), which ALSO covers the previously-uncovered retry-as-update sub-case. The target `except IntegrityError` branch was genuinely load-bearing in BOTH versions; only the comment/mechanism was inaccurate. LESSON: a "race" test that never persists a competing row tests retry-as-reinsert, not retry-as-update — assert the count the REAL race produces (2, not 1), and the assertion doubles as proof the update branch ran.

**Reviewer B's one non-reproducing enrichment failure = SHARED-WORKING-TREE contamination, NOT a real flake (run-44 hazard reconfirmed).** Reviewer B saw the enrichment test's RuntimeError escape uncaught once, unreproducible across ~135 repeats. Cause: Reviewer A was CONCURRENTLY mutating `src/enrichment/llm_workflows.py` (removing that exact try/except to test load-bearing) while Reviewer B ran the combined tests — reviewer subagents share the maker's working tree. Not a defect in the test; a 40-run isolated soak = 0 failures. LESSON (again): parallel reviewer subagents mutating source for load-bearing checks can transiently redden each other's runs; a non-reproducing "flake" during concurrent review is contamination, not the diff.

**CONSIDERED-AND-DECLINED (recorded so each is a decision, not an oversight):**
- **Backend `/api/auth/me` "missing db.commit()" (backend-correctness scout) — VERIFIED HARMLESS, declined.** `check_usage_limits` flushes a 30-day monthly-quota reset; `get_db` only closes (rollback on close), so the `/me` READ path's flush is discarded. But the scout's "quotas permanently stuck / app unusable" is FALSE: the WRITE paths (create_job → `increment_job_usage` → `db.commit()`, asgi.py ~1547) commit the reset+increment together, so the reset durably persists on the next write (re-derived from the unchanged `usage_reset_date`); `/me`'s response is computed correctly in-memory regardless, so no wrong display and no wrong enforcement. Adding a commit to a GET would be a zero-value side-effect anti-pattern. (`test_auth_usage.py` already pins the reset logic.)

### 2026-07-15 (run 53) — Same-day follow-on (after run 52 #405). FULL 7-scout sweep on a late-convergence codebase → shipped ONE honest PR = 2 file-DISJOINT value-bar changes (a webhook REPLAY-attack regression test + an honest-error fix on the demo funnel) + bookkeeping. 2 Sonnet reviewers.

- **Webhook replay-attack regression test (`tests/test_billing.py`, file-DISJOINT).** Every signed-webhook test used `_sign` (fresh `time.time()`), so Stripe's timestamp/replay-window defense was NEVER exercised — only the HMAC path was. Added `_sign_at(payload, ts)` (valid HMAC, explicit ts) + `test_webhook_rejects_replayed_ancient_timestamp_and_grants_nothing`: a correctly-signed event stamped `t=1000` (1970) must be rejected on `stripe.Webhook.construct_event`'s default 300s tolerance (`SignatureVerificationError` → the handler's `except` → 400) and grant NOTHING (tier stays FREE, no `Subscription` row). Verified locally: `stripe.Webhook.DEFAULT_TOLERANCE == 300`; the 6-test webhook slice + full `test_billing.py` (28) green; distinct from the forged-HMAC test (which fails the HMAC check, not the timestamp check). A library bump or misconfig that disabled the timestamp check would now redden per-PR instead of silently allowing captured-event replay to re-grant entitlement.
- **Demo funnel honest-error on a non-JSON 2xx (`web/app/demo/demo-client.tsx`, file-DISJOINT).** `fetchMatch` did `res.json().catch(() => ({}))`, so a 200 with an unparseable body (an edge/proxy/WAF HTML page, a stale-CDN response) silently became `{}` → `Results` rendered FAKE SUCCESS ("your résumé already covers every skill this role names") on the public, no-account aha funnel (§34). Replaced with an explicit parse that preserves the prior `!res.ok` error branch and, only on a 2xx-non-JSON, throws an honest error instead of returning `{}`. Verified: web `tsc --noEmit` + `eslint` green. **Honest severity note (not overstated):** low-severity edge case — the backend always returns JSON on 200, so this only manifests behind an interposing 200-HTML layer; kept because eliminating a fake-success dead-end on the flagship funnel is squarely the SIDE-EFFECT-INTEGRITY standard, and the fix is tiny + regression-free. Deliberately did NOT touch the identical `web/lib/api.ts:84` pattern — that shared client legitimately sees empty/204 bodies, so throwing on non-JSON there would regress real success paths.

The two ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked: business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B adoption DATA (`floor_met_year1=false`, un-gamed — no buildable lever); store-readiness needs a signed native build (screenshots) + bespoke icon (designer) + mobile IAP (native/owner). ### 2026-07-15 (run 52) — FULL 8-scout deep audit (new day; last full sweep run 50, ~24h+). 7 of 8 axes honestly clean/owner-blocked; the PERFORMANCE scout found the ONE genuine value-bar defect → shipped 1 PR = an unbounded-query fix on the dashboard hot path. Both Sonnet reviewers APPROVE (Reviewer A independently revert-verified the guard; Reviewer B verified the honesty of the display cap + flagged a fair non-blocking fast-follow, actioned as a comment-honesty tweak).

**The one genuine find — `GET /api/jobs` returned ALL jobs when `limit` was omitted (unbounded).** `list_jobs` had `limit: Optional[int] = Query(None, ge=1, le=500)` but only applied `.limit()` when `limit is not None` — so an omitted limit (exactly what web `page.tsx:35` AND both mobile clients send on every dashboard load / session restore) did an unbounded scan. Paid tiers have NO job cap (`FREE_JOBS_LIMIT` is per-MONTH; Premium = "unlimited"), so a long-tenured power user's large pipeline could load thousands of rows (+3 `selectinload` relationships each) and serialize a multi-MB response, risking the Vercel 60s budget on the hottest authed read. **Fix (`asgi.py`):** bound an omitted `limit` to `_JOBS_LIST_DEFAULT_LIMIT = 500` — the SAME ceiling an explicit `limit` is already `le=500`-capped at, so no new magic number and the omitted default == the max explicit page. The dashboard's "Tracked" total comes from the SEPARATE aggregate `/api/analytics/pipeline` `COUNT(*)`, so the display cap never distorts any count. Load-bearing test (`tests/test_perf_n1.py`): monkeypatches the cap low (3), seeds 5 jobs, asserts an omitted limit returns exactly 3 (reverting to `if limit is not None` returns 5 → reddens); asserts count not row-identity so it's immune to `created_at` tie-ordering. **maker≠checker:** Reviewer A reverted the fix in-tree and empirically confirmed the test fails `assert 5 == 3`, then restored byte-identical; Reviewer B confirmed no export/other consumer depends on receiving all rows and the "Tracked" stat stays truthful.

**CONVERGENCE READ (unchanged, ~46× re-confirmed at the build waterline).** The remaining 7 scouts (web-functional, backend-robustness, security, business-case, artifact-freshness, store-mobile, tests-eval) each returned ZERO genuine loop-buildable findings — a healthy late-convergence codebase, NOT artificial scarcity (one real defect WAS found + shipped). The two ship-critical dims stay owner/market-blocked: business-case floor $57.5K<$100K needs live B2B adoption DATA (`floor_met_year1=false`, un-gamed — no buildable lever); store-readiness needs a signed native build (screenshots) + bespoke icon (designer) + mobile IAP client (native/owner). The scorecard's LOOP-buildable A→A+ top_gaps (performance timeout #389, route-inventory #390) shipped runs 48; remaining ones need owner keys (tests-evals CI-liveness → GEMINI in CI; security → TURNSTILE_SECRET; design → native captures). Readiness honestly NOT met/attempted. No recurring wall → no harness proposal.

**NAMED FAST-FOLLOW (deferred, NOT scarcity — genuinely lower-value + can't-currently-happen at 0 users):** no client implements list pagination, so a >500-job cohort would see only the 500 most recent with no in-product "load more" (the API supports `limit`/`offset`; no client uses it). Strictly better than the timeout it replaces and the count stays honest, so it doesn't block the fix. Building pagination UI now (0 users, nobody near 500 jobs) would be speculative gold-plating; reopens when a real user approaches the cap. Reviewer B's comment-honesty nit (my first comment implied a working client escape hatch) was actioned pre-merge — the comment now states the API *capability* + names this fast-follow.

**LESSON (reinforces "verify the DATA bound, not just the code path"):** the unbounded scan looked harmless because the FREE tier caps jobs at 5 — but that cap is PER-MONTH and PAID is unlimited, so the reachable state is a large accumulated pipeline, not a single request. A "can't-happen because of the free cap" read would have wrongly dropped this; checking the paid-tier entitlement (`auth_service.py`) proved it reachable. Symmetric to run 49's lesson (a bounded-short field can't overflow) — here an *unbounded* field on the paid path CAN.

- **Stripe Billing Portal (#401 part 1 — `src/billing.py`, `asgi.py`, `web/{lib/api.ts,app/pricing,app/app/settings}`, `tests/test_billing.py`, ROUTE_INVENTORY).** Existing subscribers who tried to change plans hit a live dead-end ("contact support / email support@…") on BOTH the pricing page (400 catch) AND the Settings Plan card. LESSON: "remove the dead-end" isn't done until a real user REACHES the fix through normal navigation — verify the entry point, not just the capability.
- **AI-consent modal focus-trap a11y (#401 part 2 — `web/components/ai-consent.tsx`).** The dialog (`role=dialog aria-modal`, gates every AI feature) lacked focus-trap/Escape/focus-restore — a keyboard user could Tab out to the inert page behind. **maker≠checker (BOTH reviewers, independently) caught a REAL focus-steal bug in my first cut:** `onCancel` was a fresh closure each PARENT render, and it was in the trap effect's deps `[open, onCancel]`, so the effect tore down + re-ran on every unrelated re-render while open — restoring focus OUT of the modal then re-stealing it (a visible flicker on the golden "Turn on AI features" path, where `setBusy(true)` re-renders the host). Fixed with `useCallback`-stabilized `settle`/`handleCancel` + a latest-value `busyRef` so Escape honours in-flight `busy` WITHOUT `busy` being an effect dep. eslint then caught a ref-write-during-render → moved to `useEffect(() => { busyRef.current = busy }, [busy])`. LESSON: a callback in a `useEffect` dep array must be STABLE (useCallback) or the effect churns on unrelated parent re-renders — a focus-trap that re-inits mid-interaction is worse than none.

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT dropped the WHOLE backend-security scout + several others (no padding, no false-fix).** The backend scout's 6 "findings" ALL failed verification: rate-limiting the Stripe/RevenueCat WEBHOOKS (#2/#5) would be HARMFUL — payment providers legitimately send bursts (retries/backfills); a per-IP limit drops real payment events → missed entitlement grants (the signature/auth gate already rejects forged events cheaply, so they're correctly NOT rate-limited); `json.loads` "hangs for minutes" (#1) false (sub-second on 10MB; the 45s LLM timeout bounds the call); session IDOR (#3) self-retracted; `score_all_jobs` ceiling (#4) is an unwired hypothetical; OrgError leak (#6) hypothetical "future dev". Also dropped: the tests-evals scout's `get_session_summary` guard test (the fn has NO endpoint = unreachable), the quota-visibility test (already covered by `check_usage_limits` 0/0 + core_journey `/me` assertion), and the web scout's interview `<select>` label "fix" (the select is NESTED inside its `<label>` = valid implicit association). Mobile IAP re-confirmed owner/validation-blocked (unrunnable native code can't flip the store-readiness C — that FAIL also needs screenshots + bespoke icon + a real validated purchase). Artifact-freshness scout: clean (docs honest).

### 2026-07-13 (run 48) — Actioned a RED main-CI signal → fixed a flaky-test CLASS + 2 scorecard A→A+ top_gaps. 3 PRs shipped (#388 rate-limit flake class, #389 Margin timeout bound, #390 route-inventory completeness+guard), 0 abandoned, 6/6 Sonnet reviewers APPROVE, 2 non-blocking reviewer catches ACTIONED pre-merge.

**Trigger: main CI was RED at run-start.** The #387 (docs-only) merge commit failed `preflight`: `test_report_is_rate_limited` → `assert 429 in [200, 200, ...]`. DEEP_DIAGNOSIS: the branch run passed, the merge FAILED on an IDENTICAL (docs-only) tree → a FLAKE, not a code regression. Root cause: the fixed-window limiter keys hits by `int(time.time()//60)` (asgi.py `_consume_counter`, 60s window); the test fires 22 requests across wall-clock time, so when a 60s boundary falls mid-test the burst splits across two windows (e.g. 4+18) and neither side reaches the 20-limit → no 429 (~a few % flake). REPRODUCED locally by forcing a boundary split (all 200s, no 429).
- **#388 (§6c fix the whole CLASS, `tests/` only).** A flake-scout confirmed the SAME mechanism in 7 tests / 4 files (report, coach-suggestions, verify-purchase, 2× read-rate-limit, 2× per-user). Froze `time.time` (monkeypatch) so all requests in a test share ONE window; tightened `test_report_is_rate_limited` to pin the exact `[200]*20 + [429,429]` boundary. Determinism proven 25/25 + 20× stress. Reviewer A broke `_consume_counter` (→True) and confirmed all 7 still fail-LOUD (non-vacuous). The 900s login-lockout tests correctly LEFT (a ~5s test can't cross a 900s boundary); the 3600s/86400s ones deferred (60×/1440× lower probability, Reviewer-A-flagged, NOT this run's CI-hit class — not padded in).
- **#389 (perf A→A+ scorecard top_gap; `src/llm.py` + scorer docstring + `.env.example` + test).** The Margin telemetry emit is BLOCKING on the LLM hot path (Vercel freezes post-response threads, #369), so the per-call timeout bounds tail-latency and STACKS per LLM call. Was hardcoded 2.0s → env-configurable `MARGIN_INGEST_TIMEOUT_SECONDS`, default 1.0s, CLAMPED to [0.1, 5.0] + `inf`/`nan` guard (Reviewer-A catch: `inf` parses as a valid float and `max(0.1, inf)==inf` would re-open the unbounded-tail hole the PR exists to close). Spy-meter test proves the resolved value reaches the constructor.
- **#390 (artifact-integrity A→A+ scorecard top_gap; doc + guard test).** ROUTE_INVENTORY scattered coverage in prose and omitted real tested routes; added a Complete route→coverage matrix (ALL 49 asgi routes, coverage grep-mapped — NO invented coverage, every route already had a test) + `tests/test_route_inventory_complete.py` asserting matrix↔asgi set-equality (fails LOUD on drift — §6c/§26 makes completeness mechanical, not a one-time patch). Reviewer A mutation-tested it (single-line + multi-line + rename drift all caught); heading-anchor hardened per his non-blocking note.

**VERIFY-BEFORE-ACT dropped 1 scout over-flag (no padding):** the correctness scout flagged an unrefunded `score_daily` ceiling slot when `score_job` raises. DROPPED as DEFENSIBLE/HONEST: `score_job(use_embeddings=True)` makes REAL paid Gemini embedding calls and the except is broad, so it CANNOT distinguish provider-failure (refund-worthy) from persist-failure-after-real-spend; refunding unconditionally would violate `_consume_counter`'s explicit "an expensive LLM attempt still counts — no fake under-count." Consume-on-attempt is the honest wallet-defense; no change.

- **#380 (correctness — `src/org_billing.py` + `tests/test_org_billing.py`, file-DISJOINT).** Async payment methods (bank transfer/SEPA/ACH) complete an org checkout UNPAID; the unpaid `checkout.session.completed` branch returned early WITHOUT storing `stripe_customer_id`/`stripe_subscription_id`. The primary map back to the org on the later `subscription.*` activation is the stamped `org_id` metadata; if that metadata is ever dropped, the ONLY fallback is a stored id — so an async-payment org could be CHARGED but never activate (zero usable seats, stuck). Fix: persist the ids on the unpaid completion (still granting NOTHING — status/seats untouched) so the stored-id fallback works. Test drives the full round-trip (unpaid persists ids + grants nothing → activation event with `org_id` metadata DROPPED still activates via the stored id); revert-verified red-without-fix. Defense-in-depth on a paid-entitlement path (the codebase's own robustness standard). ### 2026-07-12 (run 44) — FOCUSED sweep (~7.5h after run 43's full deep audit; cadence-aware, NOT a re-run). **Cadence-aware scope discipline (run 41 precedent, re-applied).** Run 43 ran the FULL ~8-scout Haiku deep audit earlier TODAY (2026-07-12 04:44 UTC) on a healthy late-convergence codebase and shipped its maximal disjoint set (#361/#362/#363). HEAD unchanged since; env unchanged (GEMINI + BROWSERBASE only — re-probed: no new Stripe price IDs / analytics / ESP / Turnstile). So re-running another full 8-scout sweep ~7.5h later would only re-derive run 43's conclusion (spend discipline). Instead ran a FOCUSED 5-Haiku-scout sweep weighted at the NEWEST surface (run 43's billing/auth/pricing changes) + the named deferrals: correctness/regression · security/abuse · functional-reality (the deferred items) · tests-evals+artifact-freshness · business-case/Track-G-H buildability. **4 of 5 scouts clean/owner-blocked**; the tests-evals scout surfaced the one real find.

- **#365 (correctness/reliability CENTERPIECE — `src/billing.py` + `src/org_billing.py` + `asgi.py` + `tests/test_billing_timeout.py`, file-DISJOINT).** A genuine BUILDS≠WORKS follow-up to #361: #361 bounded every Stripe HTTP call at 25s (< Vercel's 60s budget) so a slow/hung call fails loud in-request — but the two checkout endpoints only caught `UnknownPlan`/`BillingNotConfigured`/`OrgError`, so the `stripe.error.APIConnectionError` that the bounded timeout raises escaped **UNCAUGHT → a generic 500**, even though `configure_stripe`'s docstring promises "the endpoint returns an honest error." The "hunt the uncaught throw on the paid path" DEEP_DIAGNOSIS case. Added `BillingProviderUnavailable`; catch `APIConnectionError` in both checkout functions → clean retryable **503** ("temporarily unavailable, no charge was made") in both endpoints. Catch is deliberately NARROW: genuine config errors (bad key/price → `AuthenticationError`/`InvalidRequestError`, siblings of `APIConnectionError`) still propagate to 500 — a 503 "try again" would mislead there. "No charge was made" is honest (Session.create is pre-checkout). Verified the SDK: stripe-python 7.9.0's `RequestsClient._handle_request_error` wraps `requests` Timeout/ConnectionError into `APIConnectionError` (Reviewer A independently confirmed against the installed SDK). 5 tests, mutation-proven load-bearing.
- **#366 (tests-evals — `tests/test_stripe_nobypass.py`, test-only, file-DISJOINT).** A per-PR source-scan guard modeled on the ratified LLM model-death no-bypass guard (#339): a raw `stripe.checkout.Session.create(` CALL may live ONLY in the two modules that call `configure_stripe()` first (`src/billing.py`, `src/org_billing.py`). Closes the gap that #361 only protects the TWO EXISTING call sites — a future new raw call would silently inherit stripe-py's 80s default and re-open the mid-request-kill incident, passing every other per-PR gate green.
- **maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP (a real vacuous-test defect, #366 Reviewer A, actioned → resolved):** the original Guard 2 (`"configure_stripe(" in text` whole-file check) was **vacuous for `src/billing.py`** — that file both DEFINES and calls `configure_stripe()`, so the substring is trivially present even if the checkout CALL SITE drops the bounding call; Reviewer A mutation-proved the exact #361 regression (remove `stripe = configure_stripe()` before the create) left both tests green. FIXED with a proximity check: the bounding CALL must appear within a 20-line window before each checkout call (excluding the `def` line) — re-verified it reddens on the reviewer's exact repro. **LESSON: a source-scan guard on a symbol that is both DEFINED and CALLED in the same file must check the CALL SITE (proximity), not whole-file presence — else it silently guards nothing.** (Same class as run 43's process-global-singleton test-isolation catch: a guard test that asserts against ambient file/global state can stop guarding without failing.)
- **REVIEWERS (2 Sonnet per change, 4 total):** #365 both APPROVE (A verified exception mapping/scoping/honesty against the installed SDK + revert-proved all tests; B verified the pre-change 500 path + value); their 2 non-blocking hardening suggestions (a narrow-scope pin that a config `AuthenticationError` still 500s; an org "no fake seat grant" assertion) were INCORPORATED into #365. #366 B APPROVE (genuine regression-net, not padding — #361 is one commit ago, a realized recurrence risk on the money path), A REQUEST_CHANGES → fixed (above).
- **SHARED-WORKING-TREE HAZARD (self-caught):** a Change-1 reviewer subagent ran `git stash`/`pop` in the shared checkout to test load-bearing, leaking Change-1's `billing.py` edit onto the branch-2 working tree; caught via `git status`, verified the diff was exactly the leak (no stashes remained), and `git restore`d before it could contaminate a commit. LESSON: reviewer subagents share the maker's working copy — their git operations can dirty it; verify tree cleanliness before each commit.

### 2026-07-12 (run 43) — FULL 8-scout deep audit → shipped the MAXIMAL disjoint set: 3 PRs / 4 findings (billing-path robustness, auth eager-load, /pricing Team discoverability). maker≠checker caught 2 REAL defects pre-merge (a guard-test isolation hole + a perf-scope overclaim); a scout FALSE-FIX was averted by verifying the SDK.

**DEEP AUDIT — 2026-07-12.** ~24h since the last full sweep (run 40) → ran the full ~8-scout Haiku deep audit (correctness · functional-reality+side-effects · security/abuse · tests-evals+artifact-freshness · design-taste · business-case-lever · store-readiness feasibility · perf/cost+Track-G/H). Shipped the maximal set of 3 file-disjoint PRs.

- **#361 (correctness+reliability CENTERPIECE — `src/billing.py` + `src/org_billing.py` + `tests/test_billing_robustness.py`, file-DISJOINT).** Two graceful-failure fixes bundled because both touch `org_billing.py`: (a) **Stripe sub-budget HTTP timeout** — stripe-python 7.9.0's default HTTP client timeout is **80s**, LONGER than Vercel's 60s `maxDuration`, so a slow/hung Stripe call is killed by the platform mid-request (possibly post-charge) with no response. New `billing.configure_stripe()` sets a 25s timeout via `new_default_http_client`; both checkout paths route through it. (b) **`add_member` concurrent race → 409** — check-then-insert with no catch let two concurrent adds of the same user both pass the `existing is None` check, then the 2nd INSERT violated `uq_org_member_user` → bare `IntegrityError` 500; now caught → rollback → `AlreadyInAnotherOrg` (already 409-mapped), mirroring `create_org`'s owner_id guard (#351).
- **#362 (performance — `src/auth/auth_service.py` + test).** `joinedload(User.subscription)` at the token-resolution choke-point removes a lazy +1 query for the endpoints that read `user.subscription` (`/me` on every session restore, ai-consent grant/revoke, Career+ salary-negotiation). One-to-one → single LEFT JOIN, no row multiplication.
- **#363 (business-case-strength — `web/app/pricing/page.tsx`).** Surfaced the built-but-undiscoverable **Team & Organizations** seat tier (highest-ARPA lever) on the public `/pricing` page for net-new/no-account buyers — it was reachable only from the authed `/app/team` dashboard. Distinct B2B band, CTA → `/app/team` (authed) or `/register?next=/app/team`. **HONEST copy: no invented price** (the per-seat price is owner-gated `STRIPE_PRICE_TEAM_ANNUAL`, shown by the real checkout), **no ARR claimed** (`floor_met_year1` unchanged). Was a NAMED run-42 follow-up.

- **maker≠checker EARNED ITS KEEP TWICE (both REQUEST_CHANGES were real, actioned → re-APPROVED — NOT rejections):** (1) **#361 Reviewer A — a genuine guard-test isolation defect:** `stripe.default_http_client` is a process-global singleton, so 2 of the 4 timeout tests read ambient global state and passed even with `configure_stripe()` reverted, as long as the constant-check test ran first — only load-bearing in isolation, not full-file order. Reviewer A mutation-proved it. FIX: reset the global to `None` per routing test; re-verified the mutation now reddens in normal order. **LESSON: a test that asserts against a process-global singleton must reset it first, or it silently stops guarding the regression it was written for.** (2) **#362 Reviewer B — a real honesty OVERCLAIM:** the comment/PR said "every authenticated request" benefits, but only ~4/39 authed endpoints read `user.subscription`. Rescoped the claim honestly (kept the fix — the join is negligible for non-readers). **LESSON: the value reviewer catches plausible-but-inaccurate perf/impact stories the correctness reviewer waves through; scope claims must match the code.**
- **SCOUT FALSE-FIX AVERTED (verify-before-act):** the functional-reality scout's recipe was to add `timeout=` as a kwarg to `stripe.checkout.Session.create` — but stripe-python 7.9.0's `create()` has NO such kwarg (verified via `help()`); the real mechanism is `new_default_http_client(timeout=)`. Implemented the correct one. The FINDING was real (unbounded call > budget); the scout's fix recipe was wrong — always verify the SDK before coding a suggested fix.

OWNER-BLOCKED (PENDING_OPS, unchanged): the two ship-critical C's — **business-case floor** ($57.5K<$100K; the seat tier is now sellable end-to-end on web, so crossing $100K needs REAL B2B adoption data, not more building — `floor_met_year1=false`, un-gamed) + **store-readiness** (rendered assets, mobile IAP, native captures) — plus the team/Career+ Stripe price secrets (nightly RED by design).

### 2026-07-11 (run 42) — CENTERPIECE: BROKE the 3× "defer the seat-tier surface" pattern — BUILT the seat-tier WEB management surface (`/app/team`), making the run-39 org tier user-reachable in-app. 1 file-DISJOINT feature PR (#356), 2 Sonnet reviewers; B's REQUEST_CHANGES (untested member-mgmt path) actioned before merge.

**The deferral was re-examined and overturned on new evidence — not artificial scarcity.** Runs 39/40/41 deferred the seat-tier web/mobile SURFACE (the lowest incomplete ROADMAP item) three times on one main ground: "a large web+mobile UI vertical on the REQUIRED web-E2E gate I can't reliably validate locally." This run RE-TESTED that assumption instead of inheriting it: `cd web && npm ci` **succeeds** here, `next build` + `tsc` + `eslint` run clean, and the Playwright harness (`playwright.config.ts` boots FastAPI + the Next prod build on a throwaway SQLite DB) runs FULLY LOCALLY — pointing at the pre-installed Chromium (`/opt/pw-browsers/chromium-1194`, build mismatch vs the pinned 1228 handled with a throwaway `executablePath` override config, NOT committed). So the "can't validate the web-E2E gate locally" premise that justified 3 defers was **stale** — the gate IS locally runnable. With that removed, deferring the one genuinely-buildable ship-critical follow-up again WOULD have been the artificial-scarcity failure mode (same lesson as run 39 breaking the 23× backend defer). The backend even redirects checkout to `/app/team` — a page that didn't exist — so the paid tier was literally unreachable dead code. LESSON: a "can't validate locally" defer is only valid while true — re-probe the environment each run (npm ci + a real build/test), because the premise can change.

- **#356 (business-case-strength surfacing — web-only, file-DISJOINT: `web/app/app/team/page.tsx` (new) + `web/lib/api.ts` + `web/lib/types.ts` + `web/app/app/layout.tsx` + `web/e2e/team-journey.spec.ts` (new) + `web/playwright.config.ts`).** `/app/team`: create-team → buy-seats → member roster. Owner/member split mirrors the server's `_org_payload` (members never see the roster — verified by reviewer + an E2E assertion). SIDE-EFFECT INTEGRITY throughout: every mutation awaits the real API and re-renders from the returned org payload (no optimistic success); buying seats hands off to REAL Stripe Checkout and refuses with an honest 503 notice (NO fake activation) when unconfigured; the async-webhook seat-grant delay is stated honestly, not papered over. Correctly called it padding → **dropped** it + its test + tightened the docstring. Reviewer A (correctness) APPROVE after empirically revert-testing every remaining guard (all real, no theater) + confirming the migration chain + `db.rollback()` safety (doesn't erase the pre-committed rate-limit counter) + the `_EMAIL_RE` forward-reference resolves. All three defer-grounds were addressed: (1) the feared "10-gate trust hole" was AVOIDED by design — entitlement reconciles through ONE function (`billing.recompute_user_tier`) writing the single `users.tier` gating column, so ZERO of the ~10 gates changed (a final reviewer grep confirmed line 121 is the ONLY `users.tier` writer); (2) NO ARR credited — `floor_met_year1` stays false (anti-gaming); (3) building monetization CODE is explicitly loop work (§13), and the product is mature so it didn't crowd out activation work. LESSON: a repeated defer on "can't land cleanly" is worth re-attacking when a cleaner DESIGN exists — reconcile-through-one-column beat the touch-10-gates approach the earlier feasibility scouts assumed.

Fix: gate on `status in _ACTIVE_STATUSES`. (B) Reviewer A round 1 — a **seat-cap over-provision race**: check-then-insert with no row lock could let 2 concurrent adds both pass `seats_used < cap`. (C) Re-reviewer B round 2 — a **mobile-entitlement reconciliation gap**: my `recompute_user_tier` claimed "single authority" but `src/mobile_billing.py` wrote `users.tier` directly, so a mobile-only subscriber who left an org seat would be wrongly stripped to FREE. A final round caught one doc-staleness nit (ROUTE_INVENTORY count/claim), fixed. FOUR review rounds each surfaced a DISTINCT issue — the process WORKING on a complex billing change, not thrashing (the ≤2-cycle brake's intent is anti-thrash; abandoning a 95%-correct ship-critical lever over a now-fixed latent bug would have been the worse error).

Both reviewers independently named the same WINDOW-ROLLOVER edge as a follow-up: `_refund_counter` recomputes `window_key` from `time.time()` at refund time, so a request that straddles the 86400s (midnight-UTC) boundary — consume in window N, 502 in N+1 — refunds N+1; usually a no-op, but if the user already made a legit request in N+1 it over-refunds by 1. Impact negligible (sub-second boundary, ≤+1 slot/day, not client-controllable, ceiling=25) → DEFERRED as a named follow-up (a clean fix threads the consumed window_key through, but it touches the shared `_consume_counter` used by the rate limiter + login lockout — disproportionate for a +1-slot/day edge).

### 2026-07-09 (run 36) — 8-scout sweep; CENTERPIECE: reconciled the 5th audit's ship-critical "functional-reality D (model decommissioned)" against the REAL provider — the model is UP — and built the DURABLE fix (resilient model fallback) the incident class actually needs. + login-lockout moved cross-instance. 2 file-DISJOINT PRs (2 Sonnet reviewers each, both APPROVE).

I probed the REAL Gemini endpoint with the live key THIS run and `gemini-2.5-flash` returned **HTTP 200 — it works right now** (both flagship reviewers independently reproduced this). So the model recovered (or the audit's probe hit a transient 404); functional-reality is NOT D for that reason. BUT the *incident class* is real and durable: `gemini-2.0-flash` IS genuinely dead (404 "no longer available"), Google decommissions models without notice, and the app had **no fallback** — a single pinned-model death 502s the WHOLE paid AI surface. So the right fix isn't "bump the pin" (the pin already works); it's RESILIENCE.

- **#330 (flagship, ship-critical functional-reality — asgi.py-FREE).** `resilient_chat_completion` in `src/llm.py`: tries the configured model, and ONLY on a model-not-found 404 falls back through a verified-live chain (`gemini-flash-latest` — a floating alias that can't be version-decommissioned — then `gemini-2.5-flash-lite`). Non-404 errors propagate (never mask a real outage); whole chain dead → fails loud (no fake success). Both real call sites (`llm_workflows._call_llm`, `career_coach` ×2) route through it; `.env.example` steers ops to the durable alias. **PROVEN end-to-end against the REAL endpoint:** forced a dead primary (`gemini-2.0-flash`) → recovered via `gemini-flash-latest`. Per-PR regression guard `tests/test_llm_fallback.py` (7 tests, no live key) closes the "silent model death passes every per-PR gate because the real-output evals are nightly-only" hole. LESSON: the LLM call sites were NOT in asgi.py (they're in `src/ai_coach/`, `src/enrichment/`) — so the ship-critical fix needed zero contended-file budget.
- **#331 (security A→A+ — the one asgi.py change).** Moved the per-account login lockout from an in-memory per-instance dict to the cross-instance `rate_counters` table (read-only `_peek_counter` for the gate + reuse `_consume_counter` for the increment). **Why now, when run 35 deferred it as "CAPTCHA is the real fix":** the 5th audit's security top-gap #8 explicitly named the in-memory lockout as a real gap, and it closes a DISTINCT hole the prior defer conflated away — a distributed brute-force that spreads across serverless instances never accumulated 5 failures on any ONE instance, so the in-memory lock was ~zero real defense. CAPTCHA remains the belt-and-suspenders for the *targeted-DoS* vector (documented honestly, owner-gated). Cross-instance regression guard proves a separate session sees the durable tally.

DEFERRED (named, buildable, not scarcity): **correctness A→A+** — refund the daily AI slot on a provider 502 (`check_llm_ceiling` pre-consumes; a flaky provider burns a legit user's quota). Needs asgi.py → collides with #331 this run; clean next-run item. **store-readiness C** — rendered feature graphic/screenshots are design-taste-gated (auto-generated slop would fail THE DESIGNER QUESTION); the brand icon + mobile IAP round-trip are owner/native-gated (a JS-only react-native-purchases wiring that still shows "coming soon" is grep-theater, not the real purchase flow I can't round-trip without a native build). **business-case seat tier** — the named floor-lever, but a ~530-LOC data-model→migration→endpoints vertical that deserves a FOCUSED run (and credits $0 ARR pre-launch, so it doesn't move the C this run); RE-CONFIRMED the pre-launch DEFER. **coverage floor 85→88** (actual 91.8%; standalone setup.cfg one-liner). **design-taste** native captures (owner-blocked). Functional-reality scout: 15/15 journeys green, ZERO other dead-ends.
OWNER-BLOCKED (PENDING_OPS): the two ship-critical C's (business-case floor + store assets/IAP/native). CAPTCHA `TURNSTILE_SECRET` (belt-and-suspenders on the lockout). `floor_met_year1=false` stands.
